  44. I received this eyelash curler to try out for the basis of this review. The following information, is 100% mine and my opinion alone. I have not used an eyelash curler in a long time, but all the hype these days seems to be on long beautiful lashes so thought I would try it. I have used mine multiple times and every time, I have had a nice uplifting curl to the lash. Make sure when you use this, you DO NOT have mascara already on the lash. This will cause the curler to stick to the lash. Apply your mascara after you curl, as the directions tell you. Also, being a makeup artist, I recommend using the blow dryer to heat the curler, just a tad. Only do this for a few seconds, and always test the how hot the curler is before ever placing it close to your eye. Heat allows the curl to set staying nice and perfect for the remainder of the day. I like that this curler also has the safety release latch, that easily can become detached. I have really enjoyed using this product and notice a big difference every time I do. Personally speaking, I would highly recommend this to others and also to my clients.

The trick to this is that the curler opens extremely wide, about half and inch or more which allows you to get very close to your roots. Be careful, you can pinch yourself! After positioning this against my roots I gently pump the curler for about seven seconds. I then move the curler down the lashes slightly and pinch and lift the handle slightly to bend them backwards. Note: this curler can give you the &#34;over curled&#34; effect if you push down too hard and can bend your lashes but if done properly this gives more curl than any other curler I've tried! I recommend combing out your lashes with a spoolie after curling to even out the curl. Even without mascara your eyelashes become instantly more noticeable after using this! HUGE curl!!
